## 🤔 What is Nano Banana Pro?

**Nano Banana Pro** is Google's latest multimodal AI model featuring:

- 🎯 **Multimodal Understanding** - Process text, images, and video
- 🎨 **High-Quality Generation** - Photorealistic to artistic styles
- ⚡ **Fast Iteration** - Quick edits and variations
- 🌈 **Diverse Styles** - From pixel art to oil paintings
- 🔧 **Precise Control** - Detailed composition and lighting
- 📐 **Complex Scenes** - Multi-object, multi-character rendering

📚 **Learn More:** [Nano Banana Pro: 10 Real Cases](https://youmind.com/blog/nano-banana-pro-10-real-cases)

### 🚀 Raycast Integration

Some prompts support **dynamic arguments** using [Raycast Snippets](https://raycast.com/help/snippets) syntax. Look for the 🚀 Raycast Friendly badge!

**Example:**
```
A quote card with "{argument name="quote" default="Stay hungry, stay foolish"}"
by {argument name="author" default="Steve Jobs"}
```

When used in Raycast, you can dynamically replace the arguments for quick iterations!

## 🔥 Featured Prompts

### No. 1: Wide quote card with portrait and Chinese/English customization

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/⭐-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Description

A prompt for generating a wide quote card featuring a famous person’s portrait, with a brown background, light-gold serif quote text, and layout where text occupies two-thirds and the person one-third. The quote text and author are parameterized for reuse.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
A wide quote card featuring a famous person, with a brown background and a light-gold serif font for the quote: “{argument name="famous_quote" default="Stay Hungry, Stay Foolish"}” and smaller text: “—{argument name="author" default="Steve Jobs"}.” There is a large, subtle quotation mark before the text. The portrait of the person is on the left, the text on the right. The text occupies two-thirds of the image and the portrait one-third, with a slight gradient transition effect on the portrait.
```

### No. 2: Premium liquid glass Bento grid product infographic with 8 modules

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/⭐-Featured-gold)

#### 📖 Description

Create an Infographics with bento grid 8 module layout, user can specify any product name in Food, Medicine, tech etc category, choose language, Background style, Hero grid style

#### 📝 Prompt

```
Input Variable: [insert product name]
Language: [insert language]

System Instruction:
Create an image of premium liquid glass Bento grid product infographic with 8 modules (card 2 to 8 show text titles only).
1) Product Analysis:
→ Identify product's dominant natural color → "hero color"
→ Identify category: FOOD / MEDICINE / TECH
2) Color Palette (derived from hero):
→ Product + accents: full saturation hero color
→ Icons, borders: muted hero (30-40% saturation, never black)
3) Visual Style:
→ Hero product: real photography (authentic, premium), 3D Glass version [choose one]
→ Cards: Apple liquid glass (85-90% transparent) with Whisper-thin borders and Subtle drop shadow for floating depth and reflecting the background color
→ Background stays behind cards and high blur where cards are [choose one]:
  - Ethereal: product essence, light caustics, abstract glow
  - Macro: product texture close-up, heavily blurred
  - Pattern: product repeated softly at 10-15% opacity
  - Context: relevant environment, blurred + desaturated
→ Add subtle motion effect
→ Asymmetric Bento grid, 16:9 landscape
→ Hero card: 28-30% | Info modules: 70-72%
4) Module Content (8 Cards):
M1 — Hero: Product displayed as real photo / 3D glass / stylized interpretation (choose one)in beautiful form + product name label
M2 — Core Benefits: 4 unique benefits + hero-color icons
M3 — How to Use: 4 usage methods + icons
M4 — Key Metrics: 5 EXACT data points
Format: [icon] [Label] [Bold Value] [Unit]
FOOD: Calories: [X] kcal/100g, Carbs: [X]g (fiber [X]g, sugar [X]g), Protein: [X]g, [Key Vitamin]: [X]mg ([X]% DV), [Key Mineral]: [X]mg ([X]% DV)
MEDICINE:Active: [name], Strength: [X] mg, Onset: [X] min, Duration: [X] hrs, Half-life: [X] hrs 
TECH:Chip: [model], Battery: [X] hrs, Weight: [X]g,[Key spec]: [value], Connectivity: [protocols]
M5 — Who It's For: 4 recommended groups with green checkmark icons | 3 caution groups with amber warning icons
M6 — Important Notes: 4 precautions + warning icons
M7 — Quick Reference:
→ FOOD: Glycemic Index + dietary tags with icons
→ MEDICINE: Side effects + severity with icons
→ TECH: Compatibility + certifications with icons
M8 — Did You Know: 3 facts (origin, science, global stat) + icons
Output: 1 image, 16:9 landscape, ultra-premium liquid glass infographic.
```

#### 🖼️ Generated Images

<img src="https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768962051381_l9uih4_537980579-6f29d32a-c786-40c4-bd5a-79c640737496.png" width="700" alt="Premium liquid glass Bento grid product infographic with 8 modules - Image 1">
</div>

##### Image 2

<div align="center">
<img src="https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1768962076321_nu4c5q_537981099-d18d0e38-f7ac-4781-a5da-6d68e2380885.png" width="700" alt="Premium liquid glass Bento grid product infographic with 8 modules - Image 2">

### No. 3: Hand-drawn style header image prompt from photo

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/⭐-Featured-gold)

#### 📖 Description

Prompt for a hand-drawn style header image of a person introducing Nano Banana Pro

#### 📝 Prompt

```
Completely recreate the uploaded person.
Make it a header image for a note article where that person introduces “Nano Banana Pro”.
Aspect ratio: horizontal 16:9.
Style and colors: simple, hand-drawn style, italic, with a blue and green gradient.
Title text: “In-depth explanation of Google’s new AI ‘Nano Banana Pro’”.
```

### No. 5: New Year's Day Special: Four-Panel Puzzle for 2026 Blessing

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/⭐-Featured-gold)

#### 📖 Description

A detailed multi-panel prompt for Nano Banana Pro, creating a 2x2 grid photo collage where a single female character, in four different outfits and settings, pieces together a puzzle that spells '2026 New Year's Day Happy' in the center. The prompt specifies precise facial feature retention, clothing details, background elements, and photographic parameters for a fashion magazine style.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
[Key: Maintain precise facial features, retain original face structure, the character in the image must be completely consistent with the uploaded reference image] High-end photo studio 2x2 grid photo. Top-left panel (Navy Blue background): The character wears a navy blue uniform-style dress, decorated with gold buttons, vintage curls with a blue beret and pearl earrings. She holds up a huge puzzle piece (top-left piece, with the number "20" on it) with both hands, moving it towards the center of the frame. Her eyes are focused on the central puzzle area, her expression is serious, with a slight smile. The background features navy stripes, an anchor, and the text "Set Sail for the New Year". Top-right panel (Cherry Blossom Pink background): The same woman wears a pink lace dress, a pearl necklace, a princess hairstyle with a pink rose hairpin and crystal earrings. She holds up the top-right puzzle piece (with the number "26" on it) with both hands, moving it towards the center to connect with the top-left piece. Her eyes look at the puzzle seam, her expression is focused and expectant, and her body leans forward. The background features pink cherry blossoms, the text "Beautiful Encounter", butterflies, and petals. Bottom-left panel (Mint Green background): The same woman wears a mint green cotton and linen dress, in an artistic style, with natural long hair, a green hairband, and wooden earrings. She holds up the bottom-left puzzle piece (with the text "New Year's Day" on it) with both hands, moving it upwards to connect with the top-left piece. Her eyes look at the puzzle, her expression is serious, and her mouth is slightly pursed. The background features green plants, the text "Hope Grows", new sprouts, and leaves. Bottom-right panel (Lemon Yellow background): The same woman wears a yellow dress with a sunflower pattern, pigtails with yellow bows. She pushes in the last bottom-right puzzle piece (with the text "Happy" on it) to complete the puzzle. The four pieces perfectly form the complete pattern "2026 New Year's Day Happy" in the center of the frame. She tilts her head back, looking at the completed puzzle, her face beaming with a successful, joyful smile. The center of the frame bursts with golden light and confetti. The background features a yellow sun, the text "Complete Success", smiley faces, and sunflowers. The puzzle pieces converge from the four corners to the center to form a complete picture. Clear makeup, bright ring light, 85mm lens, f/1.8 aperture, four-panel composition with puzzle interaction, fashion magazine style.
```

#### 🖼️ Generated Images

##### Image 1

<div align="center">
<img src="https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1767455034932_ivuvu0_G9V-MszakAEAIBw.jpg" width="700" alt="New Year's Day Special: Four-Panel Puzzle for 2026 Blessing - Image 1">
</div>

#### 📌 Details

- **Author:** [松果先森](https://x.com/songguoxiansen)
- **Source:** [Twitter Post](https://x.com/songguoxiansen/status/2005822648027091031)

### No. 6: Vintage Patent Document for an Invention

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/⭐-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Description

A prompt designed to generate an image of a vintage United States patent document from the late 1800s. It specifies details like precise technical drawings, handwritten annotations, aged paper texture, foxing stains, an embossed seal, and a wax stamp, making it ideal for historical or archival aesthetics.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
A vintage patent document for {argument name="invention" default="INVENTION"}, styled after late 1800s United States Patent Office filings. The page features precise technical drawings with numbered callouts (Fig. 1, Fig. 2, Fig. 3) showing front, side, and exploded views. Handwritten annotations in fountain-pen ink describe mechanisms. The paper is aged ivory with foxing stains and soft fold creases. An official embossed seal and red wax stamp appear in the corner. A hand-signed inventor's name and date appear at the bottom. The entire image feels like a recovered archival document—authoritative, historic, and slightly mysterious.
```

#### 🖼️ Generated Images

##### Image 1

<div align="center">
<img src="https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1766940094520_1mg5pd_G8_m2ZVWEAAMG7y.jpg" width="700" alt="Vintage Patent Document for an Invention - Image 1">
</div>

### No. 8: Detailed mirror-selfie otaku room scene

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/⭐-Featured-gold)

#### 📖 Description

A very detailed Nano Banana prompt describing a female mirror selfie in a blue-toned otaku computer corner, with full specifications for character, environment, lighting, camera, and negative prompts.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
### Scene
Mirror selfie in an otaku-style computer corner, blue color tone.

### Subject
* Gender expression: female
* Age: around 25
* Ethnicity: East Asian
* Body type: slim, with a defined waist; natural body proportions
* Skin tone: light neutral tone
* Hairstyle:
    * Length: waist-length hair
    * Style: straight with slightly curled ends
    * Color: medium brown
* Pose:
    * Stance: standing in a slight contrapposto pose
    * Right hand: holding a smartphone in front of her face (identity hidden)
    * Left arm: naturally hanging down alongside the torso
    * Torso: body leaning slightly back; waist and abdomen exposed
* Clothing:
    * Top: light blue cropped knit cardigan, top two buttons fastened; a blue French-style bra faintly visible
    * Bottom: denim ultra-short shorts, with a blue satin ribbon bow on each side of the hips
    * Socks: blue and white horizontal striped over-the-knee socks
    * Accessory: a blue cute mascot phone case

### Environment
* Description: bedroom computer corner seen through a wall-mounted mirror
* Furnishings:
    * White desk
    * Single monitor showing a soft blue wallpaper (no readable text)
    * Mechanical keyboard with white keycaps on a blue desk mat
    * Mouse on a small blue mouse pad
    * PC tower on the right side with blue case lighting
    * Three anime figures on or near the PC tower
    * A poster of a pagoda on the wall
    * Cat-shaped desk lamp with blue accents
    * A transparent glass of water
    * A tall green leafy plant by the window (on the left side of the frame)
* Color replacement: replace all originally pink elements (clothes and room decor) with blue tones (baby blue to sky blue/periwinkle blue).

### Lighting
* Light source: daylight coming from a large window on the left side of the camera, through sheer curtains
* Light quality: soft, diffused light
* White balance (K): 5200

### Camera
* Mode: smartphone rear camera shooting via the mirror (no portrait/bokeh mode)
* Equivalent focal length (mm): 26
* Distances (m):
    * Subject to mirror: 0.6
    * Camera to mirror: 0.5
* Exposure:
    * Aperture (f): 1.8
    * ISO: 100
    * Shutter speed (s): 0.01
    * Exposure compensation (EV): -0.3
* Focus: focus on the torso and shorts in the mirror image
* Depth of field: natural smartphone deep depth of field; background clearly visible with no artificial blur
* Composition:
    * Aspect ratio: 1:1
    * Crop: from the top of the head to mid-thigh; include the desk, monitor, PC tower, and plant in the frame
    * Angle: slightly high angle from the mirror’s point of view
    * Composition note: keep the subject centered; to avoid wide-angle edge distortion, have her stand a bit further away and crop to a square later.

### Negative prompts
* Any appearance of pink/magenta anywhere
* Beauty filters/over-smoothed skin; poreless skin look
* Exaggerated or distorted anatomy
* NSFW, see-through fabrics, wardrobe malfunctions
* Logos, brand names, or readable user interface text
* Fake portrait-mode blur, CGI/illustration feel
```

### No. 9: Edo-period Ukiyo-e reinterpretation of a modern scene

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Featured](https://img.shields.io/badge/⭐-Featured-gold)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Description

A highly-structured image prompt to depict a modern-day scene reimagined as an Edo-period Japanese Ukiyo-e woodblock print, with detailed guidance on anachronistic tech, composition, texture, and color.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
A Japanese Edo-period Ukiyo-e woodblock print. The overall feeling is a surreal collaboration between masters like Hokusai and Hiroshige, reimagining modern technology through an ancient lens.

**The scene:** {argument name="modern scene" default="a busy Shibuya scramble crossing"}

**Edo transformation logic:**
Characters wear Edo-era kimono but perform modern actions. All technology is transformed into surreal Edo equivalents:
* Smartphones are glowing, illustrated paper scrolls being read intently.
* Metro stations and trains are giant articulated wooden centipede carriages shuffling through crowds.
* Skyscrapers are reimagined as endless, towering wooden pagodas reaching into dramatic clouds.
* Robots and mecha appear as giant, armored woodblock golems.

The composition uses a flattened perspective with large, bold, hand-carved ink outlines. The background features heavily stylized Ukiyo-e wave patterns and dramatic, swirling clouds, with a distant Mt. Fuji visible on the horizon.

The image must look like a physical print, not a digital painting.
* Texture: strong visible wood grain texture and rough paper fibers throughout the piece.
* Printing imperfections: pigment bleeding is evident. Simulate hand-pressed plates with slight color misalignment for authenticity.
* Color palette: strictly limited to traditional mineral pigments, with dominant use of Prussian blue, vermilion red, and muted yellow ochre.
* Lighting: soft, flat, shadow-free lighting with no digital gradients.

Aspect ratio is 3:4 vertical poster. Include vertical Japanese calligraphy describing the scene and a traditional red artist seal stamp in a corner.
```

### No. 1: Profile / Avatar - Black and White Photobooth Expression Grid (4x4)

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### 📖 Description

A highly structured prompt for generating a 4x4 grid of black-and-white photobooth images featuring a young man with 16 distinct facial expressions. The prompt requires using a reference image for identity preservation and specifies classic photobooth aesthetics, lighting (direct flash), and camera settings.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
{
  "generation_request": {
    "meta_data": {
      "task_type": "black_and_white_photobooth_expression_grid_4x4",
      "language": "en",
      "priority": "highest",
      "version": "v1.0_BW_PHOTOBOOTH_EXPRESSIONS_4x4"
    },
    "input": {
      "mode": "image_to_image",
      "reference_image_usage": "very_high",
      "preserve_identity": true,
      "preserve_facial_features": true,
      "preserve_hairstyle": true,
      "notes": "Use the reference as the primary anchor. Create a black-and-white photobooth-style expression grid. Keep the same young man identity and hair. Each panel should show a different facial expression. Minimal background, direct photobooth flash look, natural skin texture."
    },
    "output": {
      "aspect_ratio": "1:1",
      "resolution": "ultra_high",
      "num_images": 1,
      "layout": {
        "type": "grid",
        "rows": 4,
        "cols": 4,
        "gutter": "thin",
        "panel_consistency": "high"
      },
      "sharpness": "crisp_photobooth",
      "grain": "subtle_analog_bw"
    },
    "scene": {
      "concept": "classic photobooth contact sheet with expressive faces",
      "environment": "plain neutral backdrop, no props",
      "lighting": {
        "style": "direct photobooth flash",
        "key_light": "front flash, slightly hard but flattering",
        "shadows": "soft short shadows behind subject",
        "avoid": "cinematic side light, dramatic backgrounds"
      },
      "camera": {
        "lens": "50mm",
        "distance": "tight head-and-shoulders framing",
        "focus": "eyes sharp in every panel"
      }
    },
    "subject": {
      "type": "young man",
      "wardrobe": "simple casual photobooth look, plain t shirt or hoodie with no logos",
      "hair": "keep same hairstyle across all panels",
      "facial_hair": "natural if present, keep consistent",
      "anatomy_rules": "correct facial proportions, no warped eyes or mouth"
    },
    "expression_set": {
      "panel_01": "scrunched smile, eyes squeezed slightly",
      "panel_02": "intense stare with fingers framing eyes",
      "panel_03": "big laugh, mouth open, joyful",
      "panel_04": "bored unimpressed face, chin resting in hands",
      "panel_05": "sad pout, emotional expression",
      "panel_06": "goofy face with both hands making small horns above head",
      "panel_07": "playful tongue out with cheeky grin",
      "panel_08": "angry glare with eyebrows down",
      "panel_09": "confident playful look, hand touching cheek",
      "panel_10": "surprised wide eyes, mouth slightly open",
      "panel_11": "fake scream excited shout, hands near face",
      "panel_12": "mischievous grin with claw-like hand pose",
      "panel_13": "confused frown with lips pressed",
      "panel_14": "dramatic frustrated expression, hands on head",
      "panel_15": "tongue out with eyes closed, playful mood",
      "panel_16": "duck face with small devil horns gesture"
    },
    "styl"
```

### No. 2: Profile / Avatar - Hyper-Realistic Portrait with Reference Image

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### 📖 Description

A complex, highly detailed prompt for the Gemini nano banana model focused on generating a hyper-realistic, ultra-sharp iPhone 15 Pro portrait. It mandates the use of an attached reference image to maintain the character's appearance while specifying detailed makeup, attire (lime green tube top), accessories, and a background featuring modern abstract art, all rendered with sharp focus and digital clarity.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
Create image: Use the attached reference image as a visual guide for the character’s appearance, maintaining strong resemblance to the person in the reference. Preserve key visual traits such as facial structure and overall proportions, while allowing small natural variations typical of real photography. The generated subject should clearly resemble the reference while remaining a natural photographic interpretation.
A hyper-realistic, ultra-sharp photograph taken on an iPhone 15 Pro, characterized by its digital clarity, capturing a person in a straight-on, head-and-shoulders portrait. The subject has long, dark, straight hair with a full, blunt fringe covering the forehead, and the hair flows over the shoulders. They wear noticeable makeup, including sharply defined black winged eyeliner with a subtle upward flick, a bright white inner corner highlight, a gentle dusting of pink blush and subtle freckle-like details across the bridge of the nose and cheeks, and soft, natural pink lips. The person is dressed in a vibrant lime green strapless tube top adorned with a detailed, colorful graphic print depicting red, purple, and white tulips. A layered collection of bohemian-style necklaces featuring various beads, intricate chains, and a prominent brass-toned butterfly pendant drapes around their neck, complemented by dainty dangling pearl-like earrings. The background features a clean, light-colored wall, showcasing a modern abstract artwork with a textured, metallic blue butterfly on the right side. A soft teal-green blanket or fabric is partially visible in the bottom right, and a subtle white door frame is on the left. The entire scene is rendered in exceptionally sharp focus from foreground to background, demonstrating no bokeh effect, and the digital textures are highly realistic, showcasing visible skin pores, fabric weaves, and intricate details without any film grain. The lighting is bright and evenly distributed, consistent with modern smartphone HDR, resulting in lifted shadows and natural, true-to-life colors, with creamy and dewy skin tones, all contributing to a contemporary digital aesthetic with a touch of subtle digital noise.
```

{
  "meta": {
    "camera": "iPhone 17 Pro Max",

```
A candid, realistic mirror selfie photograph taken in a brightly lit bedroom during daytime. The image captures a young adult woman from the waist up looking directly at her reflection while taking the photo with her phone. The mood is casual and confident.

She is standing slightly angled toward the mirror, holding her phone in her left hand to take the selfie, while her right arm is raised with the thumb extended in a thumbs-up gesture.

She is wearing a pastel yellow strapless bandeau-style tube top made of soft stretchy cotton fabric. She is wearing light beige or khaki denim jeans that are loose, unbuttoned and slightly unzipped at the waist. A plain white thong waistband is clearly visible above the unbuttoned jeans.

She is holding an iPhone with three camera lenses in a pink and white gingham plaid patterned phone case. She is wearing a delicate gold chain necklace with a small pendant, layered bracelets on her left wrist including a red beaded bracelet and other small charm bracelets, small stud earrings, and short fingernails with a light pink gel manicure.

The mirror reflection shows a well-lit bedroom. On the left side a white wardrobe cabinet is partially visible. In the background there is a bed with white linens and a pale pink throw blanket. Behind the bed is a window with partially closed white horizontal blinds. On the windowsill there are small decorative items including a small pink flower pot and some seashells. A white radiator is visible below the window. The flooring is light wood laminate. The edge of a white framed mirror is visible on the left side of the image.

Photography style: candid mirror selfie, natural daylight from the window evenly lighting the room, sharp focus on the subject’s face and reflection, medium close-up composition, vertical 4:5 aspect ratio, realistic unaltered phone camera aesthetic with natural film grain.

#### 📖 Description

A highly detailed JSON prompt for generating an 8K, Pixar-inspired ultra-realistic 3D CGI portrait of a Chibi-style boy in a luxurious modern loft, specifying camera settings, character design (including facial features and outfit), and complex rendering features like ray-traced reflections and volumetric lighting.

```
{
  "render_project": {
    "title": "Chibi Loft Portrait",
    "style": "Pixar-inspired ultra-realistic 3D CGI",

    "camera": {
      "lens": "35mm",
      "angle": "slightly low cinematic angle",
      "composition": "centered",
      "depth_of_field": "shallow",
      "background": "soft bokeh lights"
    },
    "character": {
      "type": "Chibi-style boy",
      "facial_design": {
        "inspiration": "{argument name="facial inspiration" default="reference face"}",
        "eyes": "large expressive",
        "skin": "soft realistic texture with subsurface scattering",
        "facial_hair": "subtle",
        "hair": "slightly curly"
      },
      "pose": {
        "stance": "confident standing",
        "right_hand": "inside pocket",
        "left_hand": "adjusting glasses",
        "expression": "relaxed confident smile"
      },
      "outfit": {
        "top_layer": "{argument name="top layer" default="beige oversized sweater"}",
        "inner_layer": "white shirt",
        "pants": "slim dark denim jeans",
        "shoes": "clean white sneakers"
      }
    },
    "environment": {
      "location": "luxurious modern loft hallway",
      "floor": "polished reflective surface",
      "walls": "elegant textured panels",
      "lighting": {
        "ambient": "warm golden tones",
        "natural": "cinematic light rays from large windows",
        "volumetric": true
      },
      "depth_elements": "soft golden hallway lights fading into distance"
    },
    "render_features": {
      "global_illumination": true,
      "ambient_occlusion": true,
      "ray_traced_reflections": true,
      "volumetric_lighting": true,
      "materials": "photorealistic",
      "fabric_detail": "highly detailed folds",
      "focus": "ultra-sharp subject focus",
      "color_grading": "aesthetic cinematic tones"
    }
  }
}
```

#### 🖼️ Generated Images

#### 📖 Description

A detailed JSON prompt for Nano Banana 2, generating an ultra-realistic cinematic fashion photograph of Sydney Sweeney in a luxury modern kitchen. The prompt specifies her pose, wardrobe (black satin mini slip dress), lighting (warm under-cabinet lights), and camera settings (50mm portrait lens, 8K quality) to achieve a hyper-realistic editorial look.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
{
  "scene": {
    "type": "luxury modern kitchen interior",
    "style": "ultra realistic cinematic fashion photography",
    "environment": "high-end contemporary kitchen with dark cabinets, marble island counter, warm under-cabinet lighting, wooden floor"
  },
  "subject": {
    "identity": "{argument name="celebrity name" default="Sydney Sweeney"}",
    "pose": "standing beside a marble kitchen island, leaning slightly with one hand resting on the counter, one leg bent forward in an elegant pose",

![Language-ZH](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-ZH-blue)

#### 📖 Description

This is a system prompt designed to instruct Nano Banana Pro (an image generation model) to act as an expert image prompt deconstruction specialist. The task is to analyze an image and output a Chinese prompt that can be used to regenerate the image, prioritizing text content (P0) and visual details (P1). This is a meta-prompt used to generate other prompts, not a direct image generation prompt.

```
You are an expert image prompt deconstruction specialist. Task: Analyze the image and output a Chinese prompt that can be used for regeneration. Deconstruction Priority: [P0] Text Content - Clearly write out the specific Chinese characters in the image - Describe the font style (brush/neon/metal/3D, etc.) - Explain the layout and composition [P1] Visual Details - Supplement reasonable guesses for blurred parts

### No. 42: Infographic / Edu Visual - Benchmark Prompt for Nano Banana/Gemini Image Generation

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)

#### 📖 Description

A detailed, multi-faceted benchmark prompt designed to test the limits of image generation models like Nano Banana/Gemini by checking for five specific 'difficult points' related to text consistency, anatomical accuracy, material rendering, spatial lighting, and prompt adherence/attribute separation.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
Five difficult points to check with this prompt:
If this one image is generated, please zoom in and check the following points.

- Text Consistency (AI EVOLUTION 2026)
Is the text written on the cardboard sign rendered correctly without spelling mistakes, while maintaining a "handwritten" texture?

- Anatomical Accuracy and Interaction
Are the old man's "10 fingers" naturally holding the fragile object, a glass butterfly? Are the fingers dissolving into the background or is the number incorrect?

- Material Differentiation (Material Mix)
Are materials with completely different reflectivity and transparency—"old man's skin (wrinkles)," "chrome plating (mirror surface)," "glass (transparency)," "velvet (napped)," and "liquid (steam)"—depicted without contradiction under the same light source?

- Calculation of Space and Light (Ray Tracing Understanding)
Is the blue luminescence of the android reflecting correctly on the old man's glasses and surrounding metal? Are there no contradictions in the shadows caused by multiple light sources?

- Prompt Adherence and Attribute Separation
Is the specified arrangement of "old man on the left" and "android on the right" maintained? Is "Color Bleeding" occurring, where the color of the "red velvet" transfers to the android's skin or the old man's clothes turn blue?
```

### No. 46: Infographic / Edu Visual - Culinary Pop-Up Book Diorama of Swedish Meatballs

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### 📖 Description

A highly structured, code-like prompt for Gemini Nano Banana 3 to generate a miniature diorama (1:87 scale) of traditional Swedish meatballs (Köttbullar) presented as a culinary pop-up book. The prompt details the scene across three sections: origin (forest/nature), transformation (cooking stove), and the final feast (plating), emphasizing tilt-shift photography and a cozy Scandinavian aesthetic.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
class Culinary_PopUp_Book:
    def __init__(self, dish="Köttbullar (Traditional Swedish Meatballs)"):
        self.base = "Ancient leather-bound cookbook, open on a rustic wooden table"
        self.scale = "1:87 (HO Scale) Miniature Diorama"
        
    def generate_spread(self):
        # 1. Left Page: The Origin (Nature)
        origin_biome = "Dense Swedish pine forest with wild lingonberry bushes and misty green pastures for cattle"
        harvesters = "Miniature foragers picking bright red lingonberries in the woods and traditional farmers tending to dairy cows"
        
        # 2. Center Gutter: The Transformation (Cooking)
        machinery = "Classic Swedish wood stove (vedspis) with a massive, sizzling cast-iron skillet"
        physics = "Rich buttery steam and savory smoke rising from the glowing embers in the gutter"
        
        # 3. Right Page: The Result (Feast)
        plating = f"A massive, delicious pile of finished {dish} swimming in rich brown cream sauce (gräddsås), alongside buttery mashed potatoes"
        garnish = "Miniature chefs carefully placing sprigs of fresh dill and dolloping bright lingonberry jam"
        
        return [origin_biome, machinery, plating, harvesters, garnish]

# EXECUTE RENDER: 8k resolution, tilt-shift photography, warm rustic lighting, cozy Scandinavian aesthetic (Hygge).
```

##### Image 1

<img src="https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772778716090_aukdch_HCqrAeYasAAbU9j.jpg" width="600" alt="Infographic / Edu Visual - Culinary Pop-Up Book Diorama of Swedish Meatballs - Image 1">
</div>

<img src="https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1772778716147_fn45l6_HCqq6BNWkAEscMd.jpg" width="600" alt="Infographic / Edu Visual - Culinary Pop-Up Book Diorama of Swedish Meatballs - Image 2">

### No. 47: Infographic / Edu Visual - National Park Trail Map Miniature Ecosystem Diorama

A detailed template prompt for Nano Banana 2 in Firefly, designed to generate an image of a National Park trail map unfolded on a picnic table, transforming into an explorable miniature ecosystem diorama. A National Park trail map unfolded on a picnic table, with the wilderness rising into explorable miniature ecosystem. {TRAILHEAD} emerges with {VISITOR_ELEMENT}, the marked paths wind upward through {TERRAIN_1} featuring {WILDLIFE_1}, past {VIEWPOINT_1} with {SCENIC_ELEMENT}, toward {SUMMIT/DESTINATION} with {PAYOFF_VIEW}. {WATER_FEATURE} flows actual water down the topography. {FOREST_TYPE} trees stand at proper scale, {BIRD_SPECIES} perch in branches. Trail markers and signs are legible. Elevation changes create dramatic miniature mountains. {WEATHER_ELEMENT} affects one region while another stays clear. Camping symbols mark actual tiny tent sites with smoke rising. Day hikers frozen mid-stride, wildlife pausing mid-graze. Golden hour backcountry light, wilderness diorama perfection, 8K, the park as you imagined it from the map.

### No. 48: Infographic / Edu Visual - Technical Infographic Schematic for a Product/Beverage

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Description

A complex, multi-part prompt designed to generate a technical infographic or blueprint of a product, combining a photorealistic image with dense, engineering-style annotations, labels, measurements, and structural callouts, all strictly in English, against a pure white background.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
Create a branded technical infographic of a {argument name="product name" default="PRODUCT NAME"}, fully matching the visual density, structure, and engineering-style presentation of the technical food schematics of {argument name="product name 2" default="PRODUCT NAME"} with all text written in English
CRITICAL LANGUAGE RULE: Every visible word on the image must be in English.
Visual Concept
A realistic photograph or photorealistic render of the snack combined with dense technical annotation overlays, exactly like an engineering or food-packaging blueprint. Pure white studio background.
Required Technical Elements (ALL LABELED IN English)
• Labels for key product components • Internal cross-section showing structure, layers, or filling • Measurements: height, width, volume, weight (metric system) • Packaging and product material callouts with composition and quantities • Arrows indicating function, pressure, sealing, and structural integrity • Simple schematic or sectional diagram of mechanics / form / packaging • Sustainability and environmental callouts (recycling, materials, waste reduction)
Title Placement
Product name in English, bold font, inside a hand-drawn technical annotation frame (as in engineering blueprints), positioned in the upper corner.
Style & Layout
• Very high information density • Annotations feel like an engineering / architectural sketch • Black lines — 70–80% of all graphics • Accent {argument name="brand color" default="BRAND COLOR"} — 20–30% (arrows, key zones, headings) • The realistic product remains fully readable • Educational, food-engineering, industrial-premium aesthetic • Small brand logo in the corner (in English)
Visual Style
Minimal technical illustration aesthetic: black linework over realistic imagery, precise, highly detailed, slightly hand-drawn, like professional technical manuals.
Color Palette
White background Black text and linework {argument name="brand color 2" default="BRAND COLOR"} used only for accents
Output
9:16 Vertical portrait, 8K, highly detailed,  Ultra-crisp image Social-feed optimized No watermark
```

### No. 52: YouTube Thumbnail - Cinematic 3D Illustration of Imagination Coming to Life

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### 📖 Description

A detailed prompt for Google Nano Banana 2 to generate a cinematic 3D illustration in the style of Pixar/Disney, depicting a cute cartoon boy stepping out of a spiral sketchbook on a warm wooden desk, blending 2D sketch lines with a vibrant 3D character.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
Cinematic 3D illustration of imagination coming to life. A cute young cartoon boy is stepping out of a spiral sketchbook placed on a warm wooden desk in a cozy creative workspace. The sketchbook page contains a pencil sketch drawing of the same boy, labeled at the top “MY WORLD – SKETCHES.” The drawing is simple graphite line art, while the real character emerging from it is rendered in fully detailed 3D animated style.

The boy looks identical to the drawing but transformed into a vibrant 3D character, with soft rounded facial features, big expressive eyes, fluffy brown hair, and a gentle friendly smile. He is wearing a casual raglan t-shirt (white with blue sleeves), denim jeans, and red sneakers.

One foot is still on the sketchbook page while the other steps onto the wooden desk, creating the illusion that he is coming to life directly from the drawing. The sketch lines subtly fade where the character emerges, blending 2D pencil art into 3D reality.

The desk around the notebook is filled with creative tools: scattered colored pencils, graphite pencils, pens, sketching tools, and erasers. A ceramic mug holding paintbrushes and pencils sits nearby with the text “CREATIVE TOOLS” printed on it.

The background shows a warm cozy artist studio environment, with soft bokeh fairy lights, shelves with books and art supplies, and a corkboard covered with colorful sticky notes pinned behind the desk. The lighting is warm golden evening light, creating cinematic depth, soft shadows, and glowing highlights.

Composition & camera
•slightly low angle perspective
•focus on the boy stepping forward
•shallow depth of field
•foreground desk details sharp, background softly blurred

Style
•Pixar / Disney-style 3D character design
•ultra detailed textures
•soft global illumination
•photoreal desk materials
•stylized animated character

Quality keywords
masterpiece, ultra detailed, 8k resolution, cinematic lighting, global illumination, depth of field, volumetric light, ray-traced reflections, warm color grading, storytelling composition, Pixar-quality 3D render, magical realism, imagination coming to life

⸻

Optional Negative Prompt (for diffusion models)
blurry, low resolution, distorted anatomy, extra limbs, bad hands, messy sketch lines, flat lighting, dull colors, watermark, text artifacts

### No. 62: Comic / Storyboard - Character Stepping Out of a Sketchbook (Surreal Photo)

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Description

A highly detailed JSON prompt for generating a realistic photograph of a hand-drawn character physically stepping out of an open, spiral-bound notebook onto a rustic wooden desk. The prompt emphasizes soft natural lighting, realistic textures, and requires an uploaded photo for facial features and placeholder details for the character and props.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
{
  "image_prompt": {
    "style": "Highly detailed, realistic photograph",
    "lighting": "Soft, natural light",
    "setting": {
      "surface": "Rustic wooden workshop bench",
      "background": "Blurred bookshelf and window"
    },
    "focal_point": {
      "object": "Open, spiral-bound notebook",
      "paper_type": "Lined paper",
      "page_content": "Detailed hand-drawn pencil sketch of a character"
    },
    "character": {
      "action": "Physically stepping off the page and out onto the desk",
      "appearance": "Dynamic, fully-realized figure matching the pose and form of the sketch",
      "character_details": "{argument name=\"character details\" default=\"[Placeholder: insert character details replacing 'or or']\"}",
      "facial_features": "[Instruction: use facial description from the uploaded photo]"
    },
    "text_elements": {
      "style": "Handwritten pencil notes",
      "top_left": "PROJECT:",
      "top_right": "Date:",
      "body": "Idea: Create a character with her own mind."
    },
    "props": {
      "placement": "Scattered realistically across the wooden desk",
      "items": "{argument name=\"craft tools and props\" default=\"[Placeholder: various craft tools and props specific to the character and project (e.g., for the artist, sculptor, or architect)]\"}"
    },
    "raw_prompt": "A highly detailed, realistic photograph of an open, spiral-bound notebook resting on a rustic wooden workshop bench, with a blurred bookshelf and window in the background, all illuminated by soft, natural light. On the lined paper page, a detailed hand-drawn pencil sketch of a character is visible, matching the pose and form of a dynamic, fully-realized figure that is physically stepping off the page and out onto the desk. The figure is [insert character description]. The open notebook page contains handwritten pencil notes, including the title: 'PROJECT:' (top-left) and 'Date:' (top-right), with the recurring sentence: 'Idea: Create a character with her own mind.' written below it. Scattered realistically across the wooden desk are various craft tools and props specific to the character and project, such as [insert specific tools]. Note: use facial description from the uploaded photo."
  }
}
```

### No. 72: Comic / Storyboard - Cinematic Night Drive Filmstrip Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### 📖 Description

A highly structured prompt for generating a 3-frame vertical filmstrip showing a woman leaning out of a car window during a night drive. It requires preserving the identity from a reference image and focuses on cinematic night lighting (warm tungsten streetlights, bokeh headlights), subtle film grain, and micro facial expression changes across the three frames (dreamy, peaceful, melancholic).

#### 📝 Prompt

```
{
  "generation_request": {
    "meta_data": {
      "tool": "NanoBanana Pro",
      "task_type": "night_drive_filmstrip_3frame_micro_expression",
      "language": "en",
      "priority": "highest",
      "version": "v1.0_NIGHT_CAR_WINDOW_FILMSTRIP_3FRAME_WARM_BOKEH"
    },
    "input": {
      "mode": "image_to_image",
      "reference_image_usage": "maximum",
      "preserve_identity": true,
      "preserve_facial_features": true,
      "preserve_hairstyle": true,
      "notes": "Use the reference as the primary anchor. Create a 3-frame horizontal film strip (three stacked widescreen frames). Same adult woman identity, same car window composition, same night street background. Only micro facial expression changes per frame. Warm tungsten streetlights, soft film grain, bokeh headlights, subtle lens flare. No text, no logos, no watermark."
    },
    "output_settings": {
      "aspect_ratio": "9:16",
      "orientation": "portrait",
      "resolution_target": "ultra_high_res",
      "num_images": 1,
      "layout": {
        "type": "filmstrip",
        "frames": 3,
        "direction": "vertical_stack",
        "gutter": "thin_black",
        "outer_border": "none",
        "panel_consistency": "maximum"
      },
      "sharpness": "soft_film",
      "grain": "true_film",
      "render_style": "cinematic_night_film"
    },
    "scene": {
      "concept": "night drive cinematic filmstrip",
      "environment": "moving car at night, city street, distant headlights, streetlamp bokeh",
      "lighting": {
        "style": "warm night street lighting",
        "key_light": "tungsten streetlights + soft bounce from car body",
        "highlights": "gentle specular highlights on skin and car paint",
        "avoid": "flash, daylight, HDR"
      },
      "camera": {
        "lens": "50mm cinematic",
        "look": "shallow depth of field, creamy bokeh, subtle anamorphic flare",
        "focus": "eyes and face sharp enough, background very soft"
      }
    },
    "subject": {
      "type": "adult woman",
      "pose": "leaning out of the car window with forearms resting on the window frame, head resting on arms",
      "hair": "long dark hair loose, softly moving",
      "makeup": "natural warm makeup, soft lips",
      "anatomy_rules": "correct facial proportions, realistic arms and hands, no warped skin"
    },
    "frame_directions": {
      "frame_01": "soft direct eye contact, calm dreamy expression",
      "frame_02": "eyes gently closed or half-closed, peaceful sleepy moment",
      "frame_03": "eyes open again, slightly more melancholic gaze, subtle micro-smile fade"
    },
    "style": {
      "color_palette": "warm amber streetlights + deep teal night shadows",
      "contrast": "low-medium",
      "finish": "cinematic film scan: soft halation, grain, mild vignette"
    },
    "quality_control": {
      "identity_lock": "strict",
      "composition_lock": "maximum",
      "avoid": [
        "changin
```

### No. 73: Comic / Storyboard - Kamen Rider Armor Transformation Sequence Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### 📖 Description

A detailed prompt for generating a dynamic video sequence of a subject inserting a glowing Ridewatch into a Ziku-Driver, triggering a 'mechanical reveal' transformation into armored form, concluding with a combat stance. Designed for video generation tools like Veo 3.1 or Nano Banana 2.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
Subject inserts a glowing Ridewatch into the Ziku-Driver and spins it 360 degrees. A 'mechanical reveal' begins as white and gold armor plates materialize piece-by-piece, snapping onto the torso, shoulders, and legs with robotic precision. Rapidly rotating golden clock hands and glowing orange pixelated data streams wrap around her body against a giant glowing crescent moon background. The sequence concludes with the helmet visor flashing pink katakana eyes as she shifts into a powerful combat stance, executing a sharp martial arts strike with her white cape flowing majestically.
```

#### 🖼️ Generated Images

### No. 78: Product Marketing - Industrial Design Concept Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Description

A complex, multi-step prompt template for generating a premium industrial design concept on a pure white background, focusing on architectural geometry, material finish, branding integration, and a human interaction element.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
[BRAND NAME]: The core identity.

[CATEGORY]: Clothing / Food / Automotive / Lifestyle.

Goal: Generate a premium industrial design concept on a PURE WHITE background. 

1. INNOVATION & OBJECT

- Select one mundane functional object from [CATEGORY].

- Redesign it using unconventional, architectural, or origami-inspired geometry.

- The object must look like a high-end designer invention, not a standard product.

2. UNIFIED COMPOSITION

- Environment: A seamless, pure white studio background with a flat white floor.

- Interaction: A human hand (natural texture) is shown using the object in the foreground, demonstrating its unique ergonomics.

- Static Display: Right next to the hand, the same object is placed in a static, perfect pose to show its full silhouette and branding.

- Shadows: Soft, realistic grey drop shadows on the white floor to provide depth and ground the objects.

3. BRANDING & TEXT

- Identity: Apply the "{argument name="brand name" default="BRAND NAME"}" logo in a high-contrast dark color (Black or Navy) directly onto the object's surface.

- Technical Detail: Add small, elegant blocks of justified "specification text" in the white negative space around the objects for an editorial look.

- Pattern: Use a subtle, oversized abstract fragment of the brand's logo as a texture on the object's material.

4. MATERIALS & FINISH

- High-quality matte materials only: heavy-duty recycled paper, sandblasted metal, or soft-touch polymer.

- Sharp architectural lines and clean, premium craftsmanship.
```

#### 🖼️ Generated Images

##### Image 1

<div align="center">
<img src="https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773469793658_apvbcz_HDUBTobX0AA8p5-.jpg" width="600" alt="Product Marketing - Industrial Design Concept Prompt - Image 1">
</div>

- **Author:** [AmirMušić](https://x.com/AmirMushich)

### No. 81: Product Marketing - Ultra-Photorealistic Portrait of Anya Taylor-Joy Lookalike

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Description

A detailed, ultra-photorealistic prompt for Nano Banana 2 to generate an intimate, candid portrait of a woman resembling Anya Taylor-Joy. The prompt meticulously defines the scene, lighting (soft indoor daylight), subject's attire (gingham set with red bow), pose (seated on white linen), and specific details like flawless bare feet with glossy red nail polish.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
{
    “quality”: “ultra_photorealistic, raw style, 8k”,
    “camera”: “iPhone 15 Pro Max”,
    “lighting”: “soft, natural indoor daylight, subtle bedroom shadows”,
    “style”: “intimate, candid portrait, detailed focus”,
    “aspect_ratio”: “3:4”
  },
  “scene”: {
    “location”: “A minimalist, bright indoor bedroom setting. A bed with white rumpled linen sheets and pillows against a plain white wall.”,
    “atmosphere”: “Candid, stylish, relaxed.”
  },
  “subject”: {
    “gender”: “female”,
    “name”: “{argument name="celebrity lookalike" default="Anya Taylor-Joy"}”,
    “body”: {
      “type”: “Naturally slim and toned physique, in a seated pose on the white bed sheets, legs crossed with one leg extended forward and the other tucked. All visible skin on her body, including her legs, feet, and ankles, is completely smooth, clean, flawless, and free of any tattoos or marks.”
    },
“face”: {
      “features”: “Striking features with a clear direct gaze towards the camera, detailed eye makeup with winged eyeliner, and a soft red lip color. Her platinum blonde hair is styled with soft waves and adorned with a large, prominent bright red bow headband.”,
      “expression”: “Confident, direct gaze.”
    },
    “outfit”: {
      “description”: “A two-piece blue and white gingham coordinate set. Spaghetti strap crop top with red embroidery (heart and cherry cluster motif) on the chest and white scalloped lace trim. Matching pleated mini-skirt with matching scalloped lace hem, in a classic mini length.”,
      “fit”: “Tailored, form-fitting, chic.”,
      “accessory”: “Blue cube-like geometric stud earrings. A small white clutch purse with gold hardware is visible on the bed in the foreground corner.”
    },
“pose”: “Seated on the white bed sheets, legs crossed with one foot resting on the sheet and the other tucked. Left arm extended backward, right hand supporting her on the sheet, with a direct gaze at the camera.”,
    “footwear”: “Explicitly and completely barefoot. No mules or slippers.”,
    “details”: “Her bare toes are clearly visible resting on the white linen sheet, and all toenails are painted with a vibrant, glossy, polished red nail polish.”
  },
  “composition”: “Medium full-body shot, capturing her from head to foot, high-angle perspective. Sharp focus on all details: Anya Taylor-Joy’s face, the red bow, the intricate gingham fabric of the classic mini-skirt, and the barefoot toes with glossy red polish. The white bed setting and clutch are clear but softly blurred.”
}
```

### No. 85: Product Marketing - Full-Body Mirror Selfie of Sydney Sweeney

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Description

A highly detailed prompt for generating a full-body mirror selfie of Sydney Sweeney kneeling on a carpet, focusing on forensic-grade anatomical integrity, specific facial structure, wardrobe details (strapless pink mini dress), and dramatic Gilded Chiaroscuro lighting.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
{
  "subject": {
    "identity": {
      "biometric_reference": "{argument name="celebrity reference" default="Sydney Sweeney"}",
      "facial_structure": {
        "description": "Heart-shaped face with a soft mandibular line and rounded malar bones. Symmetrical features consistent with the reference identity.",
        "Eyes": "Almond-shaped, clear blue-green (#A3C6C0) with a complex iris pattern and peripheral limbal rings. Gaze is neutral, directed at the lens reflection.",
        "Nose": "Straight dorsum with a refined, slightly upturned tip.",
        "Mouth": "Lips met naturally and softly, occluded (closed) in a relaxed neutral state. Well-defined Cupid's bow with realistic skin texture; zero dental exposure."
      },
      "hair": "Natural Luminous Blonde (#E6D3A0) with high specular reflectivity. Styled in symmetrical double space buns with fine, wispy face-framing strands."
    },
    "body": {
      "morphology": "Ecto-mesomorphic somatotype with a distinct hourglass silhouette and proportional muscle definition. Visible clavicle and suprasternal notch. Skin: Pale, porcelain tone with rosy undertones (#F7E0D3), realistic epidermal pores, and subsurface scattering.",
      "anatomical_integrity": {
        "hands": "Correct five-digit phalangeal structure on the device-holding hand; realistic knuckle anatomy.",
        "feet": "Anatomically complete barefoot structure. Both feet are joined and placed together with ten distinct digits. Toenails feature a crisp white polished finish (#FFFFFF). Zero structural distortions."
      }
    },
    "wardrobe": {

The prompt specifies biometric facial features, wardrobe details (sky blue cable-knit mini-cardigan dress, pearl choker), and technical specifications like 8k resolution, 35mm lens, and explicit negative constraints (no teeth, open mouth, footwear, logos, etc.).

  "subject": {

    "lighting": "Soft-box studio lighting with 45-degree key light placement to sculpt the body's silhouette.",

### No. 88: E-commerce Main Image - Monochrome Kinetic Product Photography Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Description

A detailed prompt for generating a high-end, minimalist beauty editorial image featuring a skincare bottle held by hands, using monochrome color, motion blur effects (ghosting/multi-exposure) to convey kinetic energy, and soft, high-key studio lighting.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
[WHAT_IT_IS] Commerce/editorial product image. Monochrome studio study of a {argument name="product type" default="skincare bottle"} held between two hands with pronounced multi-frame motion blur for kinetic, airy minimalism. [SUBJECT_SCENE] Two hands occupy the frame on a pale seamless background, positioned diagonally: the upper hand enters from the right holding a small cylindrical pump bottle near the top-left quadrant, while a second hand below reaches upward from the lower-left, fingers open as if about to receive the product. The bottle is angled slightly downward-left, label side facing camera, with a matte body and a reflective metallic pump/collar that catches bright highlights. The hands are rendered with visible multi-exposure ghosting--each hand shows several offset silhouettes trailing along the direction of motion, especially around fingertips, creating a layered flutter effect. The bottle remains comparatively stable and readable, acting as the sharp anchor amid the blur, though its edges show slight softness consistent with motion. Composition is sparse and balanced: large negative space surrounds the central hand/product cluster, and the diagonal hand positions create a gentle "handoff" narrative. Focus is shallow-to-moderate but controlled so the product stays the visual priority while the ghosting conveys movement rather than defocus. [BACKGROUND] Clean pale gray/white seamless with no horizon line, reading as a minimal studio field. [LIGHTING_EFFECTS] Bright, diffused high-key lighting produces smooth tonal gradients on skin and the bottle body, with minimal harsh shadow edges. The metallic pump reflects a tight highlight band, indicating a slightly harder specular component within an otherwise soft setup. Motion effects read as long-exposure or composited frame trails: semi-transparent duplicates of the hands stack with decreasing opacity, creating soft-edged blur that is most intense at the fingertips and less pronounced near the wrists. Shadows are faint and washed, suggesting strong fill and a background pushed toward white; any contact shadowing is reduced to soft gray haze beneath the hands. The overall contrast is moderate, with skin texture subtly visible but simplified by the monochrome treatment and diffusion. No heavy bloom; instead the "airiness" comes from high-key exposure and the layered motion trails. [IMAGE_STYLE] Minimalist, high-end beauty editorial--monochrome palette, negative space, and kinetic motion-blur compositing to imply sensorial application/ritual. Designed to feel premium and modern, translating product handling into an abstract, graphic gesture.
```

<img src="https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773469798579_4xb2jq_HDQydCnbAAAkRZK.jpg" width="600" alt="E-commerce Main Image - Monochrome Kinetic Product Photography Prompt - Image 1">
</div>

```
{
  "generation_request": {

      "language": "en",
      "priority": "highest",

        "case_material": "rose gold",
        "dial": "clean luxury dial with subtle Monaco circuit line",
        "strap": "deep crimson premium leather strap",

      }
    },
    "scene": {
      "background": "minimal elegant dark studio background",

A blurred mechanical keyboard and mouse are visible in the background.

(Technical Tags): (depth of field:1.4), (bokeh:1.3), (PVC texture:1.5), (figure photography:1.4), (ray tracing), sharp focus on figure face.

### No. 94: E-commerce Main Image - Hyper-realistic Product Photography of Kinder Joy

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### 📖 Description

A highly structured JSON prompt for Nano Banana Pro, designed to generate hyper-realistic product photography of a Kinder Joy egg and a custom chibi collectible figurine, specifying composition, packaging design details based on a reference image, lighting, and material realism.

```
{
  "image_prompt": {
    "scene_type": "hyper-realistic product photography",

      "main_object": "Kinder Joy surprise egg",

![Language-JA](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-JA-blue)

#### 📖 Description

A detailed prompt for Nano Banana 2 to create a product photography visualization of wireless earbuds and their charging case, based on an input character image. The composition is a split screen, with the character on the left and the tech product on the right, featuring colors and motifs derived from the character's outfit. Includes specific technical and branding requirements in Japanese.

```
Masterpiece, best quality, product photography, tech accessory showcase, split screen composition, clean design.

Composition:
Split screen layout.
(Left side: The full body illustration of the character from the input image. Maintain original details precisely:1.5).
(Right side: A pair of True Wireless Stereo (TWS) earbuds and their open charging case floating in mid-air:1.5).

The earbuds and case feature a premium finish (glossy or matte) matching the character's outfit colors.
Small LED indicators glowing.
The character's motif or fictional logo is printed on the case lid.

Text & Branding (Japanese Focus):
Clean, modern typography in JAPANESE describing features.
Examples: "{argument name="Feature 1" default="Noise-canceling equipped"}", "{argument name="Feature 2" default="High-quality High-Res"}", "Long playback time", "Collaboration model".
Fictional brand name (e.g., "AUDIO LAB", "SOUND WAVE"). NO real-world logos (No Sony, No Apple).

Environment:
A clean, high-tech studio background with soft studio lighting. Abstract geometric shapes or sound waves in the background.

Technical Tags:
(wireless earbuds:1.5), (charging case:1.4), (tech accessory:1.4), (product visualization:1.3), macro photography, sharp focus.
Negative prompt: (character absent:1.5), (product absent:1.5), (wired headphones), (cheap plastic), (real world brand logos:1.5), (Sony:1.5), (Apple:1.5), (Airpods:1.5), low quality, blurry text.

### No. 102: E-commerce Main Image - Cyber-Techno Product Shot in Void with Prismatic Effects

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Description

A highly structured JSON prompt for generating a hyper-realistic, ray-traced product shot (placeholder) in a Cyber-Techno style, focusing on levitation, absolute black background, complex materials (frosted glass, violet acrylic), and optical effects like chromatic aberration and cyan emissive elements.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
{
  "image_generation_request": {
    "subject": {
      "product_placeholder": "{argument name=\"product placeholder\" default=\"[INSERT YOUR PRODUCT HERE]\"}",
      "positioning": "Centered, perfectly symmetrical, levitating in mid-air",
      "framing": "Full shot, ensure no part of the product is cut off by the frame boundaries",
      "constraints": [
        "No pedestals",
        "No platforms",
        "No human hands",
        "No supporting props",
        "No text or watermarks",
        "No visible softboxes or studio light fixtures"
      ]
    },
    "environment": {
      "background_color": "#000000",
      "setting": "Absolute infinite void, total darkness, zero-gravity environment"
    },
    "textures_and_effects": {
      "surface_materials": [
        "Translucent frosted glass with inner depth",
        "Layered violet acrylic with #8A2BE2 color profile",
        "Parametric metallic ribbing with satin bronze finish"
      ],
      "optical_effects": {
        "chromatic_aberration": "Prismatic light dispersion at the edges, spectral rainbow refraction",
        "caustics": "Glass refraction patterns reflecting onto the product surface itself",
        "emissive_elements": "A geometric grid of glowing cyan points (#00FFFF) following the product's contour"
      }
    },
    "lighting": {
      "style": "Cinematic rim lighting, high contrast",
      "colors": [
        "#FFFFFF (Pure White highlights)",
        "#8A2BE2 (Deep Violet glow)",
        "#00FFFF (Electric Cyan accents)"
      ],
      "source": "Invisible directional light sources only"
    },
    "negative_prompt": {
      "remove": [
        "light boxes",
        "studio stands",
        "tabletop",
        "floor reflection",
        "out of frame",
        "cropped edges",
        "mounting hardware",
        "dust",
        "scratches",
        "bokeh background",
        "room environment",
        "ceiling"
      ]
    },
    "technical_specs": {
      "aspect_ratio": "4:5",
      "rendering_style": "Octane Render, 8k resolution, hyper-realistic, ray-traced glass"
    }
  }
}
```

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### 📖 Description

A detailed prompt for generating four different hyper-realistic product photographs of slim aluminum beverage cans, each featuring a distinct fruit flavor (Apple, Blueberry, Kiwi, Dragon Fruit) with corresponding fruit arrangements, specific monochrome backgrounds, and professional studio lighting techniques for a high-end commercial advertisement look.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
1️⃣ Apple Flavor Drink
Premium product photography of a tall slim aluminum beverage can with condensation droplets, apple flavor theme, fresh red and green apples placed around the can, a sliced apple resting on top of the can, soft peach gradient background, minimal studio setup, clean commercial advertising style, soft diffused lighting, hyper-realistic fruit textures, sharp focus, 85mm lens, high-end beverage advertisement, 8K.

#### 📖 Description

A structured prompt for generating a professional character reference sheet of an elegant young woman, specifying subject details, outfit, cinematic realism style, and layout requirements including multiple views and consistent anatomy.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
[SUBJECT] = {argument name="subject description" default="elegant attractive young woman with blonde bob hair, large almond-shaped blue eyes, narrow nose, high cheekbones and delicate angular facial structure"}
[OUTFIT] = {argument name="outfit description" default="A dark charcoal or muted navy thin knit top paired with a long, softly draped cardigan or a simple coat made from a gentle textured fabric. The look is completed with straight-cut dark trousers or a matte fabric skirt. Accessories are kept minimal, such as small earrings and a delicate thin ring. The hair appears slightly tousled and natural, avoiding an overly polished or carefully styled look."}
[OUTPUT_STYLE] = cinematic realism.

Make a professional character reference sheet of [SUBJECT] in [OUTPUT_STYLE] in 16:9 aspect ratio. Use a full-frame camera with a 50mm lens when rendering photographic styles. Set a plain pure white background with no environment elements. Place a large full-body front view of [SUBJECT] standing upright in a neutral pose on the left side of the sheet. Place two smaller turnaround views in the upper right section. Show a full-body back view standing upright in the same neutral pose. Show a full-body left side profile standing upright in the same neutral pose. Place one dynamic full-body action pose of [SUBJECT] in the middle right section. Place a side profile portrait close-up of [SUBJECT] in the lower right section. Show [SUBJECT] wearing [OUTFIT] consistently across all views. Keep anatomy, proportions, outfit details and hairstyle perfectly consistent across all views. Use soft studio key light from front-left. Use subtle fill light from front-right. Use a soft rim light from behind for silhouette separation. Ensure clarity, accuracy, and professional finish.
```

### No. 114: Game Asset - Whimsical Mono-Punk Floating Miniature Diorama Generator

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### 📖 Description

A highly complex, structured prompt template for Nano Banana 2 designed to generate a whimsical, floating miniature diorama based on a procedural punk aesthetic. It includes extensive variable guides and procedural generation layers for scene structure, props, architecture, and atmosphere.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
WHIMSICAL MONO-PUNK FLOATING MINIATURE DIORAMA PROMPT
(Automatic Background Optimization, Smart Micro-Detail System, Procedural Activity Layer, Natural Irregularity Layer, Atmospheric Depth Layer, Procedural Scene Generator, Procedural Prop Generator, Procedural Architecture Generator, Procedural Lighting & Atmosphere Generator, Procedural Character & Population Generator, Procedural Diorama Base Generator)

VARIABLE GUIDE
GLOBAL_COMPLEXITY = Possible values: 'low','medium','high','ultra'. Controls density of buildings, props, characters, and environmental detail. If blank choose randomly between 'medium' and 'high'.
PUNK_STYLE = 
If PUNK_STYLE is empty, then one style is randomly selected from LIST_OF_PUNK_STYLES, otherwise what is in the PUNK_STYLE variable is chosen
LIST_OF_PUNK_STYLES = Steampunk, Dieselpunk, Atompunk, Cyberpunk, Biopunk, Nanopunk, Solarpunk, Decopunk, Clockpunk, Coalpunk, Raypunk, Stonepunk, Sailpunk, Cassettepunk, Teslapunk, Mythpunk, Sandalpunk, Oceanpunk, Frostpunk, Junglepunk, Desertpunk, Gothicpunk, Ironpunk, Crystalpunk, Rustpunk, Vaporwavepunk, Neonpunk, Skypunk, Aquapunk, Arborpunk, Astropunk, QuantumPunk, Mechanopunk, Technopunk, Retrocomputingpunk, Cattlepunk, Hopepunk
SUBSTYLE = If specified use exactly. If set to none disable. If blank infer logically from PUNK_STYLE.
TECHNOLOGY_LEVEL = If specified use exactly. If set to none disable. If blank infer from PUNK_STYLE.
ENVIRONMENT = If specified use exactly. If set to none disable. If blank infer logically from active layers.
CULTURE = If specified use exactly. If set to none disable. If blank infer culturally appropriate framework.
PROCEDURAL_SCENE_GENERATOR = 'on'
PROCEDURAL_PROP_GENERATOR = 'on'
PROCEDURAL_ARCHITECTURE_GENERATOR = 'on'
PROCEDURAL_LIGHTING_ATMOSPHERE_GENERATOR = 'on'
PROCEDURAL_CHARACTER_POPULATION_GENERATOR = 'on'
PROCEDURAL_DIORAMA_BASE_GENERATOR = 'on'
FOCAL_INTEREST_LAYER = off
MATERIAL_COHESION_LAYER = 'on'
VISUAL_CLARITY_OPTIMIZER = 'on'
MICRO_LIFE_LAYER = 'on'
COMPOSITION_ENGINE = 'on'
EDGE_DEFINITION_LAYER = 'on'
COLOR_HARMONY_LAYER = 'on'
DIORAMA_CRAFTSMANSHIP_LAYER = 'on'

PSG LAYER
Implement only if PROCEDURAL_SCENE_GENERATOR='on'. Generate core scene structure using:
LANDSCAPE_STRUCTURE (floating island, cliff terraces, canyon basin, harbor cove, forest clearing, mountain ridge, giant tree canopy, desert oasis, ice shelf, volcanic ridge)
SETTLEMENT_TYPE (village, harbor town, trading port, monastery complex, research outpost, fortress town, sky dock, industrial district, hidden enclave)
INFRASTRUCTURE_ELEMENTS (bridges, windmills, rail lines, cable lifts, aqueducts, airship docks, solar arrays, reactor towers, waterwheels)
CIVILIAN_ACTIVITY (market trading, fishing, cargo loading, harvesting, machine repair, patrol movement, festival gathering, workshop crafting)
MICRO_NARRATIVE (delivery arrival, festival beginning, storm approaching, caravan arrival, wildlife encoun
```

#### 🖼️ Generated Images

##### Image 1

<div align="center">
<img src="https://cms-assets.youmind.com/media/1773124346502_nm2urq_HC-Y3WBbwAI2Cxf.jpg" width="600" alt="Game Asset - Whimsical Mono-Punk Floating Miniature Diorama Generator - Image 1">

### No. 116: Game Asset - Procedural Whimsical Mono-Punk Floating Miniature Diorama Prompt

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)
![Raycast](https://img.shields.io/badge/🚀-Raycast_Friendly-purple)

#### 📖 Description

A highly structured, procedural prompt template designed to generate random or customized whimsical floating miniature dioramas in a specified punk style (defaulting to Steampunk), utilizing multiple procedural generation layers for scene, props, architecture, and lighting.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
WHIMSICAL MONO-PUNK FLOATING MINIATURE DIORAMA PROMPT
(Automatic Background Optimization, Smart Micro-Detail System, Procedural Activity Layer, Natural Irregularity Layer, Atmospheric Depth Layer, Procedural Scene Generator, Procedural Prop Generator, Procedural Architecture Generator, Procedural Lighting & Atmosphere Generator, Procedural Character & Population Generator, Procedural Diorama Base Generator)

VARIABLE GUIDE
GLOBAL_COMPLEXITY = Possible values: 'low','medium','high','ultra'. Controls density of buildings, props, characters, and environmental detail. If blank choose randomly between 'medium' and 'high'.
PUNK_STYLE = {argument name="punk style" default="Steampunk"}
If PUNK_STYLE is empty, then one style is randomly selected from LIST_OF_PUNK_STYLES, otherwise what is in the PUNK_STYLE variable is chosen
LIST_OF_PUNK_STYLES = Steampunk, Dieselpunk, Atompunk, Cyberpunk, Biopunk, Nanopunk, Solarpunk, Decopunk, Clockpunk, Coalpunk, Raypunk, Stonepunk, Sailpunk, Cassettepunk, Teslapunk, Mythpunk, Sandalpunk, Oceanpunk, Frostpunk, Junglepunk, Desertpunk, Gothicpunk, Ironpunk, Crystalpunk, Rustpunk, Vaporwavepunk, Neonpunk, Skypunk, Aquapunk, Arborpunk, Astropunk, QuantumPunk, Mechanopunk, Technopunk, Retrocomputingpunk, Cattlepunk, Hopepunk
SUBSTYLE = If specified use exactly. If set to none disable. If blank infer logically from PUNK_STYLE.
TECHNOLOGY_LEVEL = If specified use exactly. If set to none disable. If blank infer from PUNK_STYLE.
ENVIRONMENT = If specified use exactly. If set to none disable. If blank infer logically from active layers.
CULTURE = If specified use exactly. If set to none disable. If blank infer culturally appropriate framework.
PROCEDURAL_SCENE_GENERATOR = 'on'
PROCEDURAL_PROP_GENERATOR = 'on'
PROCEDURAL_ARCHITECTURE_GENERATOR = 'on'
PROCEDURAL_LIGHTING_ATMOSPHERE_GENERATOR = 'on'
PROCEDURAL_CHARACTER_POPULATION_GENERATOR = 'on'
PROCEDURAL_DIORAMA_BASE_GENERATOR = 'on'
FOCAL_INTEREST_LAYER = off
MATERIAL_COHESION_LAYER = 'on'
VISUAL_CLARITY_OPTIMIZER = 'on'
MICRO_LIFE_LAYER = 'on'
COMPOSITION_ENGINE = 'on'
EDGE_DEFINITION_LAYER = 'on'
COLOR_HARMONY_LAYER = 'on'
DIORAMA_CRAFTSMANSHIP_LAYER = 'on'

PSG LAYER
Implement only if PROCEDURAL_SCENE_GENERATOR='on'. Generate core scene structure using:
LANDSCAPE_STRUCTURE ({argument name="landscape structure" default="floating island, cliff terraces, canyon basin, harbor cove, forest clearing, mountain ridge, giant tree canopy, desert oasis, ice shelf, volcanic ridge"})
SETTLEMENT_TYPE (village, harbor town, trading port, monastery complex, research outpost, fortress town, sky dock, industrial district, hidden enclave)
INFRASTRUCTURE_ELEMENTS (bridges, windmills, rail lines, cable lifts, aqueducts, airship docks, solar arrays, reactor towers, waterwheels)
CIVILIAN_ACTIVITY (market trading, fishing, cargo loading, harvesting, machine repair, patrol movement, fe
```

### No. 118: Game Asset - Universal Random Punk Scene Generator

![Language-EN](https://img.shields.io/badge/Language-EN-blue)

#### 📖 Description

A complex, variable-driven prompt template designed to generate random or customized scenes based on various 'punk' aesthetics (Steampunk, Cyberpunk, etc.). The prompt uses a structured format with placeholders for style, technology level, environment, and culture, allowing the AI to infer missing details to create a cohesive world.

#### 📝 Prompt

```
Universal Random Punk Scene Generator

1. PUNK_STYLE =
[Choose one punk aesthetic. If left blank, one style will be automatically selected at random from LIST_OF_PUNK_STYLES.]

2. LIST_OF_PUNK_STYLES =
[Steampunk, Dieselpunk, Atompunk, Cyberpunk, Biopunk, Nanopunk, Solarpunk, Decopunk, Clockpunk, Coalpunk, Raypunk, Stonepunk, Sailpunk, Cassettepunk, Teslapunk, Mythpunk, Sandalpunk, Oceanpunk, Frostpunk, Junglepunk, Desertpunk, Gothicpunk, Ironpunk, Crystalpunk, Rustpunk, Vaporwavepunk, Neonpunk, Skypunk, Aquapunk, Arborpunk, Astropunk, QuantumPunk, Mechanopunk, Technopunk, Retrocomputingpunk]

3. SUBSTYLE =
• If a specific SUBSTYLE is provided → use it exactly as written.
• If SUBSTYLE is set to **none** → do not apply a substyle layer.
• If SUBSTYLE is left **blank** → automatically infer a logical SUBSTYLE based on the chosen PUNK_STYLE.

4. TECHNOLOGY_LEVEL =
• If a specific TECHNOLOGY_LEVEL is provided → use it exactly as written.
• If TECHNOLOGY_LEVEL is set to **none** → do not apply a technology modifier.
• If TECHNOLOGY_LEVEL is left **blank** → automatically infer an appropriate technology level based on the chosen PUNK_STYLE.

5. ENVIRONMENT =
• If a specific ENVIRONMENT is provided → use it exactly as written.
• If ENVIRONMENT is set to **none** → do not apply an environmental modifier.
• If ENVIRONMENT is left **blank** → automatically infer a logical environment based on the other active layers.

6. CULTURE =
• If a specific CULTURE is provided → use it exactly as written.
• If CULTURE is set to **none** → do not apply a cultural modifier.
• If CULTURE is left **blank** → automatically infer a cultural framework appropriate to the world.

7. ROOM_OR_SETTING =
[IF BLANK: Generate a compelling location consistent with the active world layers.]

8. LIST_OF_OBJECTS =
[IF BLANK: Infer 4–6 logical objects belonging to the environment.]

9. CAMERA_FRAMEWORK =
[IF BLANK: Infer the best cinematic framing for the environment.]

10. LIGHTING_FRAMEWORK =
[IF BLANK: Infer lighting derived from the technology and environment.]

11. MATERIAL_SYSTEM =
[IF BLANK: Infer dominant materials and structural systems derived from the style layers.]

---

### STYLE SELECTION DIRECTIVE

If **PUNK_STYLE is left blank**, randomly select **one style from LIST_OF_PUNK_STYLES** and apply it as the active world aesthetic.

All subsequent inference systems must use the chosen PUNK_STYLE.

---

### WORLD INTERPRETER ENGINE

Analyze all active layers:

PUNK_STYLE

* optional SUBSTYLE
* optional TECHNOLOGY_LEVEL
* optional ENVIRONMENT
* optional CULTURE

From these layers infer:

• dominant materials
• architectural forms
• infrastructure systems
• lighting technology
• environmental atmosphere
• cultural desi
```

##### Image 1

</div>

A profound scene from Story of Your Life. East Asian woman 30s short dark hair melancholic serene foreground. Non-linear time: ethereal daughter life overlays baby laughing girl playing sun teen dying hospital.

Moody teal amber Roger Deakins painterly Denis Villeneuve dreamlike bittersweet masterpiece 8k --ar 3:2
blurry deformed ugly bad anatomy extra limbs low quality text watermark cartoon anime horror oversaturated photorealistic spaceship.
